[30;1m519 | [0m[35mRebasing is the process of moving a branch to a new base commit. From a content[0m
[30;1m520 | [0m[35mperspective, rebasing really is just moving a branch from one commit to[0m
[30;1m521 | [0m[35manother. But internally, Git accomplishes this by creating new commits and[0m
[30;1m522 | [0m[35mapplying them to the specified base—it’s literally rewriting your project[0m
[30;1m523 | [0m[35mhistory. It’s very important to understand that, even though the branch looks[0m
[30;1m524 | [0m[35mthe same, it’s composed of entirely new commits.[0m
